## ÔÜí EARLIER ÔÇö 2026-06-26 **PHASE H ┬Ě H5 increment 4 ÔÇö FORTIFICATIONS DEPTH COMPLETE (D142), closing the locked D138 UG:G-fidelity modern-engine push.** This is a **D74 gameplay carve-out**, not presentation-only: the modern engine now has staged entrenchments (**rifle pits / hasty cover Ôćĺ full parapet Ôćĺ redoubt / earthwork**), facing-aware works (front strongest, flank reduced, rear bypass still matters), stronger/clearer prepared abatis when tied to own parapets/redoubts, visible 2D/3D earthworks, HUD status, a player charge-impetus commit lock, and H5-i3's swamp/town/fort arrays now feed the universal T0 cover/move hooks (no per-battle fudge). **NEXT = H2 reenactment-footage decision or Phase I/J polish; Q5 Chattanooga + Q6 USCT battles remain LAST.**

Units that march off their own works lose the cover while the visible works fade. Abatis built by a brigade in its own parapet/redoubt is marked prepared, starts stronger, slows more, bites morale/disorder/fatigue harder, clears slower, and renders with clearer stakes/backing. 2D and 3D draw hasty/parapet/redoubt shapes; the HUD names the stage and front-cover multiplier; the end card teaches the Hess/Mahan fortification lesson.

AI inline charges stay unchanged. `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` now wires D141 terrain through `fldCoverAt`/`fldMoveFactor`: fort strong cover + attacker friction, town hard cover + street friction, swamp soft concealment + major slow, with the old wall/woods/hill ladder retained. This is ONE universal combat model; no scenario outcome gate.

## ÔÜí EARLIER ÔÇö 2026-06-26 **PHASE H ┬Ě H5 increment 3 ÔÇö TERRAIN READABILITY: the modern (non-hex) engine now makes high/low ground ÔÇö and EVERY topography type ÔÇö EXPLICIT (D141), the THIRD step of the locked D138 arc.** Three player-chosen **elevation modes** (default **HILLSHADE** relief = T21's, no double-count ┬Ě **CONTOURS** = iso-lines + elevation labels ┬Ě **COLOR-BY-HEIGHT** = a CVD-safe **Viridis** hypsometric tint), cycled from the in-battle settings drawer + the **R** key + the legend's mode chip; an **always-on compact LEGEND** (mode chip ┬Ě viridis gradient ┬Ě a live **on-hover elevation+type readout** ┬Ě a topography key of the types present); the 2D top-down finally shows relief it never had; and **swamp / town / fort** are now distinct render types. All PRESENTATION-ONLY Ôćĺ byte-identical. The hex engine IS Classic ÔÇö untouched.

> **ÔşÉ THE i3 DISCIPLINE (read first ÔÇö the SAME as i2, NOT the i1 carve-out).** PRESENTATION-ONLY, held to the FULL D74 byte-identity law. NEW `src/tactical/T22-terrain-readability.js` wraps the render seams BY ASSIGNMENT (fld3dInit / fld3dBuildTerrain / fld2dInit / fldPointerMove / fldExit; carries the ._wx/._atmo/._rr/._vf markers forward), reads-only, never writes sim/`fldRng`/`_SAVE_VER`. The elevation mode is a sim-UNREAD `G.settings.fldElevMode` (the renderRich pattern ÔÇö kept in `G.settings` only, NOT localStorage, so the documented "hillshade" DEFAULT holds every fresh session). The new **swamp/town/fort** terrain arrays (`__FIELD.terrain.swamps/towns/forts[]`) are **combat-INERT ÔÇö read by NO sim/combat function** (a probe static-scan enforces it), so combat stays byte-identical even though terrain was ADDED Ôćĺ proven `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff + `probe-bullrun` 15/15.
>
> **WHAT SHIPPED (D141) ÔÇö T22 (Ôëł630 lines) + thin T0/T6 seams.** (1) **3 modes**: HILLSHADE (3D = T21's slope-AO relief, T22 adds NOTHING to the 3D ground here so relief is never double-counted; 2D paints its own cached hillshade ÔÇö the top-down had none); CONTOURS (a 3D `LineSegments` of marching-squares iso-lines + elevation-label sprites; 2D = offscreen-cached polylines); COLOR-BY-HEIGHT (a 3D viridis-tinted overlay mesh; 2D = cached viridis canvas). The 3D hypso+contour are PREBUILT once and `.visible`-toggled per mode (snappy, no rebuild, no camera jerk). (2) **Legend + hover** ÔÇö `#fldElevLegend` (mode chip ┬Ě viridis gradient bar ┬Ě `#fldElevHover` live readout ┬Ě topography key). (3) **swamp/town/fort** distinct in 2D + 3D (swamp = wet-teal disc + reeds; town = clustered buildings; fort = angular earthwork berm + bastions); a demo set in the sandbox showcase. T0 seams: `fldBuildTerrain` gains the demo arrays; `fld2dDraw` calls the guarded `fldTrDrawGround2d` after the field fill; `fldKey` gains the `R` branch. T6: the drawer gains an "Elevation display" cycle control.
>
> **AARON'S 3 FORKS (AskUserQuestion):** palette = **Viridis** ┬Ě legend = **always-on compact panel** ┬Ě topography = **add swamp/town/fort** (visual-now / sim-cover-wiring-later ÔÇö that's what keeps i3 byte-identical).
>
> **BUG-HUNT (43 agents, 6 lenses ├Ś 3-skeptic refute + completeness critic):** 4 confirmed of 12 raw + 2 critic-new, **ALL FIXED before commit:** (perf) the 2D contour mode re-stroked ~600ÔÇô1600 segments EVERY frame Ôćĺ now rendered ONCE to an offscreen canvas (2 batched strokes) + blitted; (a11y MED) the legend mode/collapse buttons dropped keyboard focus to `<body>` on the innerHTML rebuild Ôćĺ focus restored in the click handlers; (MED) the legend topography key + height-range went STALE on a phase advance Ôćĺ a topography-aware legend signature now refreshes on any terrain change in BOTH renderers; (LOW) dropped the localStorage round-trip; (LOW) removed a redundant double-dispose of the cloned hypso mesh; (LOW) the per-pointer hover classify early-outs on a coarse cell; (robustness) the base-called 2D hook gained a full-body try/catch. ## ÔÜí EARLIER ÔÇö 2026-06-23 **Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER ÔÇö seat your generals into the DIVISION billets nested under each corps; a corps is only as good as its divisions** (overnight run, D110 ÔÇö Codex code + Claude vetting/doc close-out)

> **The GM depth-chart's next rung is shipped** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬ž12.1 ÔÇö Army Ôćĺ Corps Ôćĺ **DIVISION** Ôćĺ Brigade), built on the Q10 corps chart (D108). Beyond seating IÔÇôIV Corps, the President now SEATS pool generals into each seated corps's **3 DIVISION billets**, spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the existing GM currency). A division can be staffed ONLY under a SEATED corps (the real chain of command), so the depth chart is a TREE built top-down. Teaches that a corps was only as good as its divisions ÔÇö A. P. Hill's "Light Division" and Hood's/Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions in Hancock's II Corps**.
>
> **ÔÜá PROVENANCE ÔÇö this milestone was a CODEX HAND-OFF, closed out here.** The Q12 CODE + DATA + PROBE were authored in an interrupted Claude-Code session and **finished + committed (`7b64d2e`) + pushed by Codex** ÔÇö a sound, builds-`GATE OK`, byte-identical-to-source feature ÔÇö **but Codex ran NO adversarial bug-hunt and wrote NO doc trail** (D110 was absent from DECISIONS/HANDOFF/WAKE-UP/RUN-LOG/V1-CHECKLIST/RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN). This session is the **close-out**: ran the missing bug-hunt, fixed its one finding, and wrote the full doc trail. **No code reverted** ÔÇö the commit is sound; the follow-up adds vetting + docs + one copy fix.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (byte-identical until you seat a division; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated division commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership` ÔÇö an INPUT the bridge already reads ÔÇö via `_cmdDivLift` = clamp(╬ú(`effDivRating`Ôłĺ64)├Ś0.03, ┬▒2). `effDivRating` = the general's GM OVR (carries the Q9 promotion) minus a `belowGradePenalty` (4) when his grade is below the **preferredGrade** ÔÇö a division was a **Maj. Gen.'s** billet in BOTH armies (distinct from the corps tier where a CS corps was a Lt. Gen.'s), so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads stretched until promoted. The lift is deliberately SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4) so the hierarchy holds: **army ┬▒17 > corps ┬▒4 > divisions ┬▒2.** No division seated Ôćĺ ╬ú over zero slots Ôćĺ lift 0 Ôćĺ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf`. **ONE BILLET PER MAN** (army/corps/division mutually exclusive; seating-higher clears the division); **vacating a corps CASCADES** (orphaned divisions stop contributing lift ÔÇö enforced at the READ layer `cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift`, cleaned on load-sanitize). `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:id}}` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered record on load. Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + capital (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG. `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand` (Inferred + 2 sources: Glatthaar, Weigley).

## ÔÜí EARLIER ÔÇö 2026-06-23 **Q10: THE CORPS DEPTH-CHART ÔÇö seat your generals into corps command over the Order-of-Battle tree; who you place (and whether his rank fits the billet) shapes how well the whole army fights** (overnight run, D108)

> **The GM depth-chart MOVE is shipped, built on the D106 OOB tree** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬ž12.1/┬ž12.2/┬ž12.4 ÔÇö "an army version of waiver/trading/transfer"). Beyond appointing the ARMY commander (the existing `cmdAppoint` billet), a new President's-Desk **"The Corps Command ÔÇö Depth Chart"** section lets the President SEAT pool generals into the army's CORPS billets (IÔÇôIV Corps), spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` ÔÇö the existing GM currency, no new resource). Each billet shows its seated commander (name + grade + OVR + a below-grade tell) with a Vacate control, or "Vacant" + a pool `<select>` + a Seat control (gated on capital); a live read-out shows the net leadership the staffed corps add. Teaches real command organization ÔÇö Lee's First (Longstreet) and Second (Jackson) Corps vs the Army of the Potomac's churning corps commands; the rout of Howard's XI Corps at Chancellorsville.
>
> **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose the depth-chart MOVES (option A) over the symmetric AI-GM (option B, flagged [hard]) because A extends the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote` spine over the D106 substrate and is byte-identical-until-moved like Q9; the new officer-slot/vacancy concept the derived T15 corps lacked is the `cmd.corps` slot map + a side-aware grade-fit.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated corps commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership(C)` ÔÇö an INPUT the bridge already reads ÔÇö via `_cmdCorpsLift(C)` = `clamp( SUM over seated slots of (effectiveCorpsRating Ôłĺ 64) ├Ś perSlotWeight, ┬▒liftCap )` (0.05 / cap 4). `effectiveCorpsRating` = the general's GM OVR (carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (6) when his CURRENT grade is below the **SIDE-AWARE** preferred grade. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership Ôćĺ bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`). The army commander still weighs most (~┬▒17); the corps lift (┬▒4) is a secondary modifier (┬ž27).
>
> **THE SIDE-AWARE GRADE-FIT (historically precise; the Q9 synergy):** a US corps was a **Maj. Gen.'s** command, a CS corps a **Lt. Gen.'s** (the CS authorized the Lt. Gen. grade Sept. 18, 1862, promoting Longstreet/Jackson that Oct. to command the ANV's new corps). So on the shipped roster only CS **Stuart** (a Maj. Gen.) seats below grade over a corps; promoting him to Lt. Gen. (Q9) removes the penalty. `data/ratings.json` `corpsCommand`: `slots 4 ┬Ě seatCost 3 ┬Ě preferredGrade {US:"Maj. Gen.",CS:"Lt. Gen."} ┬Ě perSlotWeight 0.05 ┬Ě liftCap 4 ┬Ě belowGradePenalty 6 ┬Ě Inferred ┬Ě 2 sources`.
>
> **BYTE-IDENTICAL until you seat a corps:** no corps seated Ôćĺ lift 0 Ôćĺ `commandLeadership` unchanged Ôćĺ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `2d11bd7` (a vacant billet contributes 0, NOT a penalty). `cmd.corps` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop invalid slots/ids/dead generals/the army commander; one corps per general; arrayÔćĺ{}). The army commander can't double-hold (excluded from the pool; `cmdAppoint` clears his corps). The seated commanders also NAME the player's DERIVED corps on the OOB board (pure display ÔÇö the predicted edge is UNCHANGED; the enemy is never named; a "Garrison" node is never named).

## ÔÜí EARLIER ÔÇö 2026-06-23 **Q8b: THE CAVALRY RECONNAISSANCE ÔÇö "scout the enemy" tier-reveals the enemy Order of Battle, scaled by your appointed general's cavalry** (overnight run, D107)

> **The camp loop's deferred SCOUTING (┬ž15) is shipped, built on the D106 OOB board.** An **"Order a reconnaissance"** control inside the Command-desk Order-of-Battle board lets the President spend a small amount of **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` ÔÇö the existing GM currency, also spent by appoint/promote; no new resource) to reveal the **enemy** order of battle to a TIER scaled by the appointed army commander's persona **`cavalry`** attribute. **Three tiers (┬ž15):** **light** (unscouted ÔÇö the passive D106 estimate: force grade band + rough count + the CTA) Ôćĺ **better** (scouted, cavalry < 65: the enemy commander NAMED + per-corps grade + a posture/terrain advisory, no per-brigade detail) Ôćĺ **full** (scouted, cavalry Ôëą 65: the complete enemy OOB). With the 9 generals' cavalry, Grant (66) + Lee (70) Ôćĺ full, the rest Ôćĺ better; a no-appointee campaign uses the HISTORICAL DEFAULT commander's cavalry. Intel is **fresh per engagement** (the scout record is keyed to the next-battle id Ôćĺ reverts to light when the battle changes). Teaches cavalry-as-the-army's-eyes ÔÇö Stuart's rides, and the Gettysburg intelligence vacuum when his cavalry was absent (a real Confederate command failure, not glorified).
>
> **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose scouting over the GM depth-chart MOVES (both unblocked by D106) because its scaling input (the `cavalry` persona attribute, spread 50ÔÇô70) + its `reveal` hook in `fldCampaignOOBHtml` BOTH already existed, `36-camp.js` explicitly deferred scouting to exactly this substrate, the D106 board already advertised a dead "Scout the enemy" CTA, and scouting is **pure display + an economy spend (never touches combat)** ÔÇö the safest byte-identity. The corps-billet MOVES need a new officer-slot concept the derived T15 tree lacks ÔÇö deferred next.
>
> **ARCHITECTURE (the D106 wall preserved):** the WRITE `cmdScout` (`src/35-command.js`) gates on capital like `cmdAppoint`, reads the appointee's cavalry via `_cmdGenPersona`, computes the tier via the pure `_cmdScoutTierForCavalry`, and writes ONLY `cmd.scout` + debits capital ÔÇö never the scoreboard. **T15-oob.js stays a PURE READ-OUT** ÔÇö `fldCampaignOOBHtml(C, {reveal, reconHtml})` is told the tier + the recon-control HTML by `cmdRenderTab`; T15 only ADDS the "better"-tier renderer (`_fldOOBSideScouted` + `_fldScoutPosture`). **No combat/resolve/tick/conditioning path reads `cmd.scout`** (grep-confirmed) Ôćĺ a campaign that never scouts is byte-identical to the pre-Q8b build, and the 9 tactical battles are untouched. `cmd.scout` rides the save (C.president serialized wholesale); `cmdInit` sanitizes a malformed/tampered record (dropÔćĺnull; validÔćĺbounded) ÔÇö no `_SAVE_VER` bump. Data: a `scout` block in `data/ratings.json` (cost 3 ┬Ě cavalryFullThreshold 65 ┬Ě baselineCavalry 54 ┬Ě 2 real sources). Build-gate 4d already scans both `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`. NO RNG.

## ÔÜí EARLIER ÔÇö 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-6 (citation-provenance) ÔÇö the CATALOG-WIDE citation hardening + a permanent build-gate** (overnight run, D103)

> **The citation-grade non-negotiable is now machine-enforced, catalog-wide.** Before you can hand a brigade a combat-biting negative badge keyed to a documented flaw, that flaw must be properly sourced ÔÇö so this milestone shipped the prerequisite to R-6's negative-badge assignment. **An audit found the "Verified-with-<2-sources" debt was NOT just badges (the logged D98ÔÇôD101 framing) ÔÇö it was 47 records across SIX data files** (badges 13 ┬Ě personas 2 ┬Ě weapons 9 ┬Ě artillery 9 ┬Ě engineering 8 ┬Ě terrain 1 ┬Ě cabinet 5). All now carry **Ôëą2 independent, real, web-verified sources**. PURE METADATA + a little teaching-card text Ôćĺ **byte-identical sim** (all 10 deterministic battles IDENTICAL to committed HEAD `5b12916`; **no numeric combat field touched**, bug-hunt-confirmed).
>
> **THE KEYSTONE ÔÇö a permanent build-gate (`tools/build.mjs` gate 4e):** recursively scans every `data/*.json`; any record whose `prov`/`provenance` is "Verified" (matched **trim+case-normalized on EITHER key** ÔÇö so a `"Verified "` whitespace/case variant OR an `Inferred`-masks-`Verified` pairing cannot erode it) carrying a `sources`/`src` array of <2 Ôćĺ `die(5)`. **Verified firing on all 47 before the fix; passes after** (`GATE OK ┬Ě parse Ôťô ┬Ě hex Ôťô ┬Ě collision Ôťô ┬Ě no-fudge Ôťô ┬Ě citations Ôťô`). The ~72 long descriptive forms ("Verified specs (ÔÇŽ)", "Verified (high) ÔÇö ÔÇŽ") cite inline in prose and trim-lowercase to Ôëá "verified", so they stay out of the structured gate **by design**. This mirrors the 4d no-fudge wall: a non-negotiable made un-erodable by the build.
>
> **THE CITATION WORKFLOW (the ultracode pattern):** 15 Opus agents ÔÇö 7 domains Ôćĺ per-domain finders Ôćĺ **default-refute** adversarial verifiers Ôćĺ a completeness critic; sources **web-checked**; discipline = NEVER fabricate, **downgrade-to-Inferred over guess**. **Zero fabrication** (critic-confirmed); all citations real/on-claim/independent. ## ÔÜí EARLIER ÔÇö 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM Q9 ÔÇö the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE: promote ┬Ě multi-currency ┬Ě merit gate)** (overnight run, D102)

> **The first real GM *move* beyond appoint/relieve is shipped.** On the President's-Desk Command tab there is now an **"Officer Corps ÔÇö Promotions"** section: the President promotes a general one grade up a clean strategic ladder (**Brig. Gen. Ôćĺ Maj. Gen. Ôćĺ Lt. Gen. Ôćĺ General**), spending a **multi-currency** budget ÔÇö **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary, shared with relief/appointment) **+ a NEW seniority pool** (`cmd.seniority`, accrues over the campaign, capped) ÔÇö and **merit-gated** by reputation. PURE INPUT-SEEDING + display, **byte-identical until the player promotes** (sandbox + all 9 battles proven byte-for-byte identical to committed HEAD `fc1d251`). Built on the existing `cmdAppoint`/`_cmdReliefCost` spine + the R-5 `fldPromotePerson` latent-command concept; entirely in `src/35-command.js` (the "Q9 (D102)" block) + a `promotion` config in `data/ratings.json`.
>
> **THE MERIT GATE (the honest history, the keystone):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep Ôëą bar) Ôćĺ a confidence bump (+3 rep); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) Ôćĺ a ├Ś1.8 capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation HIT (Ôłĺ4)**. Because OVR = 0.55┬Ěskill + 0.45┬Ěreputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** ÔÇö rank without merit doesn't make a good commander (teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence). Leapfrogging a passed-over senior adds a seniority surcharge.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path, no fudge):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small **BOUNDED** amount ÔÇö `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase grade-delta ├Ś 0.92), clamped to **ÔëĄ6** ÔÇö added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating Ôćĺ commandLeadership Ôćĺ` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). `cmdPromote` writes ONLY `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation` ÔÇö **never the scoreboard** (D74/D94 wall). **0 lift when un-promoted Ôćĺ every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical** (live-sanity proven: a promotion stores "Lt. Gen.", lifts commandLeadership 79Ôćĺ80; the un-promoted skill reads identical with/without C for all 20 generals).
>
> **New fns (`src/35-command.js`):** `_cmdPromoCfg`/`_cmdRankBase`/`_cmdBaseGrade`/`_cmdGradeIdx`/`_cmdNextGrade`/`_cmdCurrentGrade`/`_cmdPromoteSkillLift`/`_cmdLeapfrogged`/`_cmdPromoteInfo`/`cmdPromote`/`_cmdPromoRow`/`_cmdPromotionsHTML`/`_cmdNum`; EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen,C)` (+lift), `cmdInit` (seeds + load-clamps `seniority`, seeds `promotions`), `cmdOnResolve` (accrues `seniority` ÔÇö invisible/byte-identical), `cmdRenderTab` (+section), `cmdWireTab` (+promote buttons); call sites `_cmdGenRating`/`cmdActiveTraits`/`_cmdActiveCard` now thread C. **Data:** the `promotion` block in `data/ratings.json` (ladder ┬Ě meritBar ┬Ě capitalCost ┬Ě aboveMeritMul ┬Ě seniority{CostBase,Leapfrog,Start,PerTurn,WinBonus,Cap} ┬Ě earnedRepBonus ┬Ě aboveMeritRepHit ┬Ě skillLiftWeight ┬Ě skillLiftCap ┬Ě topCommandPreferredGrade).
>
> **Bug-hunt (7 Opus agents: 4 diverse-lens finders ├Ś default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 2 raw Ôćĺ 2 confirmed + 1 actionable critic gap, ALL LOW + LATENT; 0 HIGH/MED; critic: "SOUND, may commit ÔÇö no-fudge/byte-identity/bounding/determinism/no-exploit all hold; no HIGH/MED missed").** ALL 3 fixed: (1) `cmdPromote` gated on `round(capital)` but spent raw Ôćĺ now debits the rounded `cap` (one lens; byte-identical under integer paths); (2) `_cmdBaseGrade`'s unrecognized-rank fallback "Maj. Gen." would over-grade a future non-named officer onto the General ladder Ôćĺ now "Brig. Gen." (lowest; hardens the deferred depth-chart path); (3) `cmdInit` now re-clamps a tampered/stale out-of-band `seniority` to the cap on LOAD. The critic's 4th note (the two `diag-classic` 404s) is the pre-existing documented tolerated asset-layer noise, not Q9.
>
> **Vet:** GATE OK (no-fudge Ôťô); `probe-command` **25/25** (9 new Q9 steps incl. the save-tamper LOAD re-clamp + the byte-identity micro-assert); **byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** vs committed HEAD `fc1d251` + Q9 live sanity (0 pe); `probe-ratings` 19/19 + `probe-desk` 13/13 + `probe-camp` 8/8 + `t1probe` 14/14 (0 pe each); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` ok; `wcag-auditor` 0 AA failures (fixed the new warning text `#c2502e`Ôćĺ`#d66040`, 4.51:1). **ENV:** the `load` suite stalled intermittently on the THREE-CDN headless load (documented gotcha ÔÇö cleared by a fresh threaded server + retry); the `domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness (`.tmp/q9-verify.mjs`, base `.tmp/q9-base.html` = `git show HEAD:civil_war_generals.html`) is the authoritative no-regression proof.

## ÔÜí EARLIER ÔÇö 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-5 ÔÇö the PROSOPOGRAPHY SCALE-OUT (bulk per-person rows + lazy materialization + play-as-anyone)** (overnight run, D101)

> **The D93 "Soldier's Story" substrate the whole rating spine was built for is shipped.** A brigade can now be inspected down to its men, any person *materialized* + *promoted*, and a generated soldier carries a deterministic name + Inferred rating ÔÇö all **PURE DATA + DISPLAY**, **byte-identical** (no shipped scenario assigns bulk persons; sandbox + all 9 battles proven IDENTICAL to committed HEAD `84c5e95`). Selecting a brigade now shows its **MEN OVR** (the men's prosopography mean) beside the R-2 combat OVR, with a provenance-hatched accent.
>
> **THE LAZY-MATERIALIZATION KEYSTONE (┬ž8) ÔÇö the whole point of R-5:** a brigade TOKEN carries ONE aggregate `fldMenMeanOVR(u,year)` (its men's mean OVR, derived **O(1)** from xp + arm-branch + year + a deterministic per-brigade-id jitter, clamped [20,88] ÔÇö a brigade AVERAGE never reaches the Legendary individual ceiling). Per-person rows are **NEVER instantiated en masse:** `fldMaterializePerson(spec,year)` builds exactly ONE row on demand; `fldBrigadeMuster(u,n,year)` a **HARD-CAPPED (ÔëĄ6)** representative sample (captain/sergeant/private from `data/ratings.json` `musterTemplate`) ÔÇö **never `u.men` rows** (proven: a 100,000-man brigade still materializes 3). The mean is always recomputable, never the source of truth (so a future zoom-to-regiment is a roll-up of materialized rows).
>
> **New pure functions (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`, the R-5 section):** `fldMenMeanOVR` ┬Ě `fldMaterializePerson` (reuses R-0 `fldDerivePerson` Ôćĺ headline + dual OVR + grade; generated Ôćĺ deterministic synth period name [`_fldSynthName`/`_FLD_FIRST`/`_FLD_LAST`, NO RNG] + Inferred + a `latentCommand` seed; authored Ôćĺ Verified pass-through) ┬Ě **`fldPromotePerson(person,toRank)`** (the latent-command **play-as-anyone** promotion ÔÇö lifts command/tactical/discipline/charisma by the rank-base delta; returns a NEW person, pure) ┬Ě `fldPersonTeam` (the EA-style {side,army,corps} journey hook) ┬Ě `fldProvenanceStyle` (the **Inferred-vs-Verified visual distinction** ┬ž10 ÔÇö Verified SOLID / Inferred **HATCHED** `repeating-linear-gradient` / Disputed dashed; meaning rides pattern + glyph [Ôťô/~/?] + word, NOT colour Ôćĺ CVD-safe) ┬Ě `fldMusterHudLine` (the live compact line) ┬Ě **`fldMusterRollHtml`** (the full "Muster Roll" panel ÔÇö probe-vetted + ready for the journey-mode character sheet / Army Register). **Live wiring = ONE guarded line** in `fldRenderHud` (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`). NO new combat path; NO RNG.

## ÔÜí CONTINUE HERE ÔÇö 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM Q8 ÔÇö the between-battle CAMP LOOP (drilling + progression)** (overnight run, D100)

> **The agency that GROWS your rating over a campaign is shipped.** A new **"Camp" desk tab**: between battles the President DRILLS the army (4 foci ÔÇö musketry/maneuver/entrenching/endurance ÔÇö each toward a ceiling, costing fatigue; or **DELEGATE** to the field officer for a steady auto-sim gain) and reads the army's drill grade + the sitting general's OVR growth (PROGRESSION ÔÇö his reputation already evolves in `cmdOnResolve`). PURE INPUT-SEEDING (no scoreboard), and **byte-identical until the player engages the camp** ÔÇö proven, committed, pushed.
>
> **`src/36-camp.js` (new module):** `campInit` (idempotent; `C.president.camp` = drill{4 foci}, fatigue, delegate, **engaged**) ┬Ě `campDrill(C,focus)` (raises a focus toward CEIL 90, +fatigue, sets engaged) ┬Ě `campSetDelegate` ┬Ě **`campTrainingBonus(C)` (THE BRIDGE SEAM** ÔÇö per-facet deltas, ALL ZERO when no focus is drilled) ┬Ě `campOnResolve` (rest sheds fatigue; a delegated army auto-drills; a clean win SEASONS / a battle this side bled the lion's SHARE erodes ÔÇö gated on `engaged`) ┬Ě `campRenderTab`/`campWireTab`. **Drilling/progression only ÔÇö SCOUTING deferred to Q8b** (needs the strategic-next-battle Ôćö tactical-OOB mapping; logged).
>
> **The bridge seam (`src/85-battle-bridge.js`):** drilling lifts firepower (musketry) / morale (maneuver) / supply (entrenching) + relieves fatigue (endurance) + a small overall sharpness ÔÇö **bounded** (full-drill Ôëł +8 overall, ÔëĄ14; fatigue DRAGS it) ÔÇö EXACTLY 0 when undrilled Ôćĺ byte-identical. Wired: `campInit` in `_t1InitAll` (after cmdInit), `campOnResolve` in `_t1Resolve` (after cmdOnResolve), the "Camp" tab in `30-president-shell.js`, `"36-camp.js"` in the manifest. `C.president.camp` rides `serializeSave` + lazy-migrates via campInit ÔÇö no `_SAVE_VER` bump.
>
> **THE KEYSTONE (byte-identity):** an `engaged` flag (false until the first drill/delegate) makes the WHOLE loop inert until the player opens the Camp (`campOnResolve` early-returns; `campTrainingBonus` is all-zero at zero drill) ÔÇö a campaign that never camps conditions byte-for-byte as the pre-Q8 build. NO RNG (deterministic).
>
> **Bug-hunt (21 Opus agents, 15 raw Ôćĺ 1 confirmed MED + 4 critic), ALL fixed:** the real one ÔÇö the "bloody" attrition test divided a raw men-count by `C.manpower.strength` (a 0-100 INDEX, also read *post-attrition*), so nearly every battle read "bloody" Ôćĺ the **win-seasons branch was DEAD** (drilled training only ever decayed, inverting the headline progression). FIXED to the casualty **SHARE** (own / both-sides total ÔÇö unitless, order-independent; PIVOT 0.55), + the probe SEASONING step re-tooled to realistic casualties + a pyrrhic-win case. Plus: removed dead `lastTurn`; corrected an overstated comment; logged that drilling is a deliberate player-only lift (the AI doesn't drill; ┬ž27-bounded).
>

## ÔÜí CONTINUE HERE ÔÇö 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-4 ÔÇö the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" surge, inside the no-fudge wall)** (overnight run, D98)

> **The Madden layer now SWINGS a fight ÔÇö provably without ever touching the scoreboard.** An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and surges on ONE channel, hard-capped. Demonstrated: a single `foot_cavalry` badge on one CS sandbox brigade **flipped a deterministic US win into a CS win** (same seed), yet the total-casualty shift was only **17.2%** and the command aura peaked at **0.47 < the 0.9 wall** ÔÇö the rating reaches the result EMERGENTLY through bounded inputs, never by writing `cas`/`victory`/`men`/`sev`.
>
> **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), `_fldXFactorInZone` tests activation (march_vigor=moving ┬Ě his_offensive=moving/charging ┬Ě ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging ┬Ě last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) ┬Ě usct_assault/mass_assault=charging ┬Ě flanking=cav & charging). In the zone it surges **ONE channel = the declared lever**: a NON-speed X-Factor sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a SPEED X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT also surge the aura. One-shot ÔÜí `fldAnnounce`+`fldScenarioBanner` (`_xfOn` rising edge); `_xfGlow` marker pulse; deterministic `_fldXfDecay`Ôćĺ1 out of zone. **NO RNG.** A unit with no X-Factor is wholly untouched Ôćĺ byte-identical.
>
> **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` ÔÇö pushes the summed aura toward the **0.9 wall, never beyond**; strict no-op unless active. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (aura summed first), gated on `badges` (NOT officers) so both surge channels share one gate.
>
> **Seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** `fldSimStep` runs the surge + apply around `fldOfficersStep`; **`fldMoveFactor` clamps the COMBINED speed factor** (the `_spdMul` surge ├Ś the R-3 static speed-badge factor) to ONE documented band **[0.75,1.30]** (exactly 1 Ôćĺ skipped Ôćĺ byte-identical); `fld2dDraw` draws a guarded `_xfGlow` ÔÇö a CVD-safe amber burst RING (the shape carries meaning) + a **vector-drawn** lightning bolt (no emoji-font tofu), `reduceMotion`-honored. **Data:** added `first_with_the_most` (Forrest, cav) Ôćĺ 7 X-Factors; none assigned to a shipped roster yet (R-6) Ôćĺ byte-identical.
>
> **Vet:** GATE OK (no-fudge Ôťô); `probe-ratings` **17/17** (the R-4 surge step + the NO-FUDGE REPLAY GATE: the surge bites + bounded + capped); the **`domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** (sandbox + 9 battles, R-4 build vs committed R-3 HEAD ÔÇö the authoritative X-Factor-off no-regression proof); `tactical-visuals` 10/10 scenes 0 pe; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; the 9 battle probes + field + logistics + bootprobe passed via `load` (when momentarily healthy). **ÔÜá ENV (still intermittent):** the standard `load` suite stalled on the THREE CDN this session ÔÇö the systems probes (officers/command/presets/ÔÇŽ) were `load`-blocked, but the byte-identity harness exercises the full `fldSimStep`Ôćĺ`fldXFactorStep`Ôćĺ`fldOfficersStep` path (officers ON) for all 10 and proves it byte-identical, covering their core concern. **Re-run them next session once `load` is healthy** (serve via ThreadingHTTPServer; if `load` still stalls, the durable fix = domcontentloaded+settle in the probe runner OR vendor THREE locally ÔÇö a recommended small vetted milestone). **Bug-hunt** (23 Opus agents, 16 raw Ôćĺ 4 confirmed + 3 critic, 0 HIGH, all LATENT@R-6): all 7 fixed (combined-speed clamp; cmdBonus surge gated to non-speed [one channel/badge]; apply decoupled from officers; vector bolt; grand_charge provÔćĺInferred + dual-downside deferred-note); catalog-wide badge-provenance sweep logged for R-6.

## ÔÜí CONTINUE HERE ÔÇö 2026-06-21 **CHICKAMAUGA ÔÇö the 3-phase Western epic shipped + adversarially hardened** (the woods Ôćĺ Longstreet's breakthrough Ôćĺ Thomas at Snodgrass Hill; probe 18/18) ÔÇö D90

> **Chickamauga is playable and verified ÔÇö the bloodiest battle of the Western theater, the fourth multi-phase epic, built on the T8 engine.** A new **ÔÜö BATTLE ÔÇö CHICKAMAUGA (1863)** main-menu button (rank 60, after Vicksburg) opens the side-choice card; command Bragg/Longstreet's army or Thomas's defense across three sectors in sequence: **P0 The Battle in the Woods (Sep 19)** ÔÇö a confused meeting engagement in blind timber; the Union line holds the road (historical). **P1 Longstreet's Breakthrough (Sep 20)** ÔÇö the Wood gap order pulls a US division out of line at the moment Longstreet's column strikes the Brotherton farm; the CS pours through and routs the right (the decisive **scoreWeight-3** phase). **P2 The Rock of Chickamauga** ÔÇö Thomas holds Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge until dusk, reinforced by Granger/Steedman, saving the army. Anti-Lost-Cause: **contingency over genius** (a staff blunder + a timing coincidence, not martial superiority) and **the squandered victory** (Bragg fails to pursue Ôćĺ the siege of Chattanooga Ôćĺ the November reversal).
>
> **Framing (decide-&-log, no fork):** the C2 "Chickamauga/Chattanooga" item = a matched PAIR of separate 3-phase epics (the Antietam/Gettysburg precedent), each its own milestone. **Top-level `attacker: CS` / `defender: US` across all 3 phases** (the Army of the Cumberland fought on the defensive) ÔÇö the CS player is the offensive, the US player holds. This sets **Chattanooga up as the US-offensive MIRROR** (the next milestone; design brief at `.tmp/chattanooga-design.md`, which also banks the engine-grain lessons from this build). Universal gun model only; **no per-battle damage fudge** (D74).
>
> **Balance (AI-vs-AI, 32 seeds, deterministic):** P0 US-holds 32/32 (mutual bloodbath ~2,400 each); P1 **CS breakthrough 32/32** (US routed cheaply, US:CS ~5.1); P2 **US-holds 32/32**, CS attacker pays **CS:US ~3.0** (the Fredericksburg failed-assault lesson); **aggregate CS 32/32** (CS 3 / US 2). A human US player who closes the Wood gap in P1 **overturns** the battle (the alt-history hinge). The CS won the field yet **bled MORE in aggregate** (~70k vs ~63k / 8 seeds) ÔÇö the costly-victory teaching, probe-guarded.
>
> **Research+verify (Workflow) corrected before authoring:** Hood Sep 20 / Maj. Gen. (not Sep 19 / Lt. Gen.); Helm under Breckinridge (not Cleburne); Cheatham restored; Granger & W.H.T. Walker = Maj. Gen.; Loring removed; gap-reporter flagged (Kellogg vs Bond); "River of Death" shipped only as disputed legend.
>
> **Bug-hunt (10 Opus agents): 2 confirmed + 3 critic, all fixed.** HIGH (the Vicksburg wrong-rank-under-Verified class): **Charles Harker was a COLONEL at Chickamauga, not "Brig. Gen."** (like Hans Heg; the BG dated to the battle but came after) Ôćĺ corrected to **Col. Harker** + a fact-check guard. Plus 4 probe-rigor guards (P1 casualty-direction US:CS Ôëą2.5, P0 winner Ôëą7/8, P1 win-by-SEIZE "hold", aggregate winner-bled-more).
>
> **Verification:** GATE OK; `probe-chickamauga` **18/18**, 0 pe; full no-regression GREEN (all 8 battle baselines + roster 8 + field/officers/logistics/arms/presets/csplayer/campaign-link/fog/ai/autopause + **custom-builder 9** [EXPECTED baseline updated for `chickamauga` ÔÇö the D86/D88 gotcha] + engineering-corps 22 + **tactical-visuals 10 scenes incl. live Chickamauga 2D/3D, texWarn 0**; diag-classic nonBlank 346; boot/t1 ok; 0 pageerrors); WCAG inherited-AA (no new color CSS). ## ÔÜí CONTINUE HERE ÔÇö 2026-06-21 **ENGINEERING CORPS ÔÇö increment 3: PONTOON BRIDGING shipped + hardened Ôćĺ THE CORPS IS COMPLETE** (the pontoon train; player-only/byte-identical; probe 22/22) ÔÇö D89

> **The Tactical Engineering Corps is DONE ÔÇö all 3 of Aaron's locked "all of the above" (entrench + abatis + pontoons).** A NEW **opt-in river** (`__FIELD.terrain.rivers[]`) actually gates movement: a river is impassable except at a **crossing** ÔÇö a **shallow ford** (passable, slow + fatiguing), a **deep ford** (fordable only at Arcade; needs a bridge at Balanced/Historian), or a player-laid **pontoon bridge** (key **N** / "Pontoon" button): an infantry pioneer detail on the near bank lays a bridge over realism-scaled time, opening a fast crossing. Surfaced via the **Skirmish Ôćĺ Ground Ôćĺ "River crossing"** option (+ an `opts.river` sandbox flag for the probe). The **B-5 realism slider** scales sapper speed, ford slow, AND fordable-vs-requires-pontoon; the strategic **Engineer Works Corps** (`bridgeArmy.engineering`) lays bridges faster on a campaign launch (the A1 anchor, via `__FIELD.engCorpsSpeed`). 2D slate-water band + boat-deck pontoons + ford stepping-stones + labels (CVD-safe, reduceMotion-safe); 3D water plane + pontoon boats/deck; a citation-grade Fredericksburg/Rappahannock + James-River-1864 teaching card.
>
> **Architecture (byte-identical):** the active gate REUSES the two T0 seams reserved for it ÔÇö `fldEngMoveFactor` (ford slow) + `fldEngMoveGate` (returns a clamped bank point for an illegal water step). New T13 fns: `fldEngInstallRiver`, `fldEngCrossAt`, `_fldRiverNearest/_fldRiverBankPoint/_fldEngBridgeSite`, `fldSelPontoon`, the pontoon loop in `fldEngStep`, `fldEngDrawWater2d`, `fld3dBuildWater` + pontoon sync in `fld3dSyncEng`. **No shipped scenario declares `terrain.rivers` and the AI never lays a pontoon** Ôćĺ every AI-vs-AI baseline byte-for-byte unchanged (every read gated by `rv && rv.length` / `engPontoons`; reset per-launch + per-phase). One T0 seam edit: `fldStepMovement` now settles a no-progress river clamp to HOLD (the bug-hunt's soft-deadlock fix) ÔÇö `eg`-gated, so riverless baselines are identical.
>
> **DECISIONS (decide-&-log, no fork surfaced):** Bull Run's creek/Stone Bridge stay COSMETIC (making them live would regress a shipped, probed battle + break byte-identity); the active river is the opt-in feature, and the teaching card cites the Rappahannock as the historical anchor. AI river-pathing / AI-built works is the named T13 extension point (player-tool this increment, like D87/D88), so a river skirmish frames the PLAYER as the attacker forcing the crossing (river installed between the player's home edge and the objective, either side) while the AI defends the far bank.
>
> **Bug-hunt (19 agents, Opus): 8 confirmed + 6 critic, all fixed.** HIGH: the gate's origin test let a unit on an open ford **sidestep into deep water and wade the band** Ôćĺ block entering blocked water from anywhere except already-blocked water + a midpoint sample (tangential bends). HIGH: the **3D water plane was buried under the opaque terrain** Ôćĺ raised to a thin on-ground sheet (+ fords lifted, no z-fight). HIGH: a unit ordered across impassable water **marched in place forever, fatigueÔćĺ100** Ôćĺ settle to HOLD at the bank. HIGH: the river skirmish was degenerate for a CS player Ôćĺ river placed by player side. MED: silent crossing refusal Ôćĺ aria-live halt announce + HUD line. LOW: dupe-span message; pontoon `side` + per-side cap.
>
> **Verification:** build GATE OK; `probe-engineering-corps` **22/22**, 0 pe; full no-regression **GREEN (21 probes byte-identical: field 13 ┬Ě bullrun 15 ┬Ě shiloh 29 ┬Ě malvern 24 ┬Ě antietam 16 ┬Ě fredericksburg 22 ┬Ě chancellorsville 24 ┬Ě gettysburg 16 ┬Ě vicksburg 18 ┬Ě roster 8 ┬Ě visuals ok [texWarn 0] ┬Ě custom 9 ┬Ě fog 13 ┬Ě ai 15 ┬Ě autopause 13 ┬Ě campaign-link 16 ┬Ě officers 15 ┬Ě logistics 14 ┬Ě arms 23 ┬Ě presets 26 ┬Ě csplayer 16; diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; boot/t1 ok; 0 pageerrors)**; WCAG-AA on all new UI (Ôëą4.5:1, CVD-safe). ## ÔÜí CONTINUE HERE ÔÇö 2026-06-18 Custom Battle Builder C4 complete Ôťů ÔÇö single-phase authoring, import/export, slots, launch gate green

> **Custom Battle Builder C4 is built and verified.** New `src/tactical/T11-custom-battle.js` adds a first-class main-menu builder flow for player-authored real-time tactical scenarios. It covers scenario name/date/place, sides/briefs, objective, field size, terrain hills/woods/walls/markers, OOB units, artillery/gun counts, reinforcement/deployment timing, optional leaders, supply trains, teaching cards, provenance, JSON import/export, shareable JSON, and six local persistence slots.
>
> **Architecture decision:** C4 is intentionally **single-phase V1**. Phase authoring remains deferred until a UI for `phases[]` can be proven as safe as authored historical phase data. Custom scenarios do **not** enter `fldScenarioRegistry()`; `fldScenarioData(id)` only falls back to `fldCustomScenarioData(id)` for explicit `custom_...` IDs. That preserves the exact historical battle roster while still launching valid custom scenarios through the same single-phase `fldScenarioInit` data path. Field size is reset every launch via `FLD.BASE_FIELD_W/H`, then a scenario may apply `field.w/h` safely.
>
> **Validation guardrails:** required metadata, safe unique IDs, malformed/unsafe JSON keys, duplicate IDs, bounds and numeric clamps, objective placement, reinforcement timing, side ownership, leader attach ownership, realistic artillery crew counts (12-40 per gun), forbidden combat/damage keys, and `phases[]` are all blocked. Custom artillery uses the universal `guns` model only; no per-custom-battle damage fudge was added.
>
> **Focused probe:** `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` verifies builder render, validation failures, valid scenario creation, export/import round trip, UI malformed-import rejection, slot save/list/load/delete, explicit custom-ID launch contract, universal gun model, field-size reset, no phase leak, no Classic `G.battle`, and no historical registry contamination. Current result: **9/9 steps ok, 0 fail**, with `tools/shots/probe-custom-battle-builder.json/png`.
>
> **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` Ôćĺ GATE OK; `node tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` Ôćĺ 9/9; `node tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` Ôćĺ 8/8; `node tools/probe-field.mjs` Ôćĺ 13/13; `node tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` Ôćĺ 15/15; `node tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` Ôćĺ 24/24; `node tools/probe-antietam.mjs` Ôćĺ 16/16; `node tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` Ôćĺ 22/22; `node tools/probe-chancellorsville.mjs` Ôćĺ 24/24; `node tools/probe-gettysburg.mjs` Ôćĺ 16/16; `node tools/probe-shiloh.mjs` Ôćĺ 29/29; `node tools/probe-officers.mjs` Ôćĺ 15/15; `node tools/probe-logistics.mjs` Ôćĺ 14/14; `node tools/probe-arms.mjs` Ôćĺ 23/23; `node tools/probe-presets.mjs` Ôćĺ 26/26; `node tools/probe-csplayer.mjs` Ôćĺ 16/16; `node tools/probe-campaign-link.mjs` Ôćĺ 16/16; `node tools/probe-tactical-visuals.mjs` Ôćĺ 6/6; `node tools/bootprobe.mjs` Ôćĺ ok=true with known/tolerated 404 resource console entries; `node tools/t1probe.mjs` Ôćĺ ok=true; `node tools/diag-classic.mjs` Ôćĺ Classic paints, nonBlank 346; `git diff --check` Ôćĺ clean.

## ÔÜí CONTINUE HERE ÔÇö run k (2026-06-16): **PHASE C-1.5 ┬Ě THE UNIVERSAL ARTILLERY GUN MODEL Ôťů SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** Ôćĺ IMMEDIATE NEXT = ANTIETAM as the MULTI-PHASE epic (D74 #1/#2)

> **The D74 "universal-combat" artillery cleanup ÔÇö the FIRST Antietam sub-milestone (do FIRST) ÔÇö is complete** (DECISIONS **D75**). Fredericksburg's per-battle **"volume-of-fire proxy men"** fudge (the C-1/D73 batteries inflated `men` to 500/440/500 to fake the massed crest fire) is REPLACED by a CONSISTENT gun-count model used identically in every battle. Deliverable Ôëł**1749.6KB**.
>
> **Ôťů THE GUN MODEL (T5):** `FLDA.GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT` = 27 (men-equivalent fire-strength per gun, UNIVERSAL). `fldArtFireStr(u)` returns the fire-strength numerator (`fldResolveFire` divides by 1500): a battery with a GUN COUNT Ôćĺ `guns * 27 * clamp(men/maxMen)` (rated fire from the gun count, crew-scaled so a battery fades smoothly as cannoneers fall); infantry / arms-off / a LEGACY no-`guns` battery Ôćĺ `u.men` EXACTLY as before. `guns` carried dataÔćĺunit via `fldMakeUnit` (T0) + `fldBrSpec` (T1); wired at `fldResolveFire`'s `strF`. CALIBRATED so a 6-gun battery Ôćĺ 162 Ôëł Bull Run's realistic 160-men/6-gun Griffin & Ricketts Ôćĺ the model REPRODUCES the existing batteries (consistent, not merely gated). The gun count is army-size-invariant "hardware" (strategic strength flows through the Cannon-Corps `_canisterScale`, not raw volume ÔÇö documented).
>
> **Ôťů BYTE-IDENTITY:** the gun path is reached ONLY by a battery declaring `guns` (Fredericksburg's 3 crest batteries); every baseline has none Ôćĺ `fldArtFireStr` returns `u.men` Ôćĺ byte-identical. **field 13 ┬Ě bullrun 15 ┬Ě fog 13 ┬Ě autopause 13 ┬Ě ai 15 ┬Ě campaign-link 16 ┬Ě officers 15 ┬Ě logistics 14 ┬Ě presets 26 ┬Ě csplayer 16 ┬Ě arms 23** ÔÇö all byte-identical, 0 pe; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14; diag-classic **346**.
>
> **Ôťů FREDERICKSBURG RE-TUNED VIA HONEST DESIGN (not fudge):** the 3 batteries now carry real gun counts (Washington Artillery 9 ┬Ě Marye's grand battery 16 ┬Ě Alexander 9 = **34 historical guns**) + realistic crew (200/350/200). The CS edge EMERGES from the wall's cover + the massed gun count + the cautious-attacker-dies-exposed geometry. RE-VET: **CS 8/8**, casualty ratio **2.06:1** (better than the proxy's 1.91), the wall measurably **load-bearing** (cuts CS loss 18-23%, 5/5 CS wins), the crest guns **survive 8/8** + fire ÔÇö **probe-fredericksburg 22/22, 0 pe**. Bug-hunt: **0 confirmed finder bugs + 5 critic gaps ALL FIXED** (the `u.men0` probe typo Ôćĺ maxMen; a battery-survival guard; a crew-scaling assertion; the campaign-semantics + legacy-HUD notes). WCAG clean.
>

## ÔÜí CONTINUE HERE ÔÇö run k (2026-06-16): **PHASE C-1 ┬Ě FREDERICKSBURG (Marye's Heights) Ôťů SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** Ôćĺ NEXT = the next Eastern marquee battle (Antietam or Gettysburg, D69)

> **C-1 ÔÇö Fredericksburg, the SECOND data-driven tactical battle ÔÇö is complete** (DECISIONS **D73**). The tactical engine (mature after B1ÔÇôB6) is now BATTLE-AGNOSTIC: a new historical battle = a `data/<battle>.json` file + one registry line, NO new combat code. New `data/fredericksburg.json` + `tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` + the T1/T7 data-driven scenario-UI generalization + a small gated T0 engine seam. Deliverable Ôëł**1743.6KB**.
>
> **Ôťů C-1 ÔÇö the data-driven scenario spine + Fredericksburg:** `fldScenarioRegistry()`/`fldScenarioData(id)` (T1) map any id Ôćĺ `GAME_DATA.<battle>`; `fldScenarioInit` builds ANY registered id from the same shape (Bull Run byte-identical). The UI is generalized: `fldInjectScenarioButtons` iterates the registry (Bull Run keeps its bespoke marquee button; others build from `data.menu`) and returns the last button so the skirmish/preset buttons anchor after the block; `fldLaunchBattle` fires the briefing for ANY scenario; `fldScenarioSideChoice(id,go)` reads `sd.sides` (a per-battle side-choice card; `fldBullRunSideChoice` is now an alias); `fldBriefObjectiveHtml` keeps the keyword skeleton + a data flavor (`sd.brief`); `fldScenarioEndHtml` keeps the Bull Run branch byte-identical (shared `_fldScenarioEndBox`) + a data `sd.endNote` branch. `bullrun.json` gained inert `sides`/`brief`.
>
> **Ôťů THE DOOMED-FRONTAL-ASSAULT POSTURE (the headline mechanic ÔÇö a scenario-gated T0 seam):** the B-1 attacker AI is *competent* (fog-off it column-rushes + presses the mass bayonet), which Fredericksburg's assault was NOT. `data.assaultDoctrine:"cautious"` Ôćĺ `__FIELD._atkCautious` makes the AI attacker advance IN LINE across the open glacis and trade but never column-rush nor carry the wall (Burnside's piecemeal disaster). `var aggressive = !__FIELD.fog && !__FIELD._atkCautious` gates the assault/column branches Ôćĺ **default off Ôćĺ Bull Run/sandbox/skirmish/campaign BYTE-IDENTICAL.** A HUMAN Union player is unbound (the alt-history hook). Fredericksburg keeps **fog OFF** (the morning fog had LIFTED ÔÇö clear fields of fire) and wins the defense by the cautious posture + the stone wall (cover 1.7) + massed crest canister ÔÇö a DIFFERENT, battle-faithful lever from Bull Run's fog (no contradiction of "fog aids the defender").
>

## ÔÜí CONTINUE HERE ÔÇö run k (2026-06-15): **PHASE B-3 ┬Ě IN-BATTLE LOGISTICS Ôťů SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** Ôćĺ NEXT = B-4 distinct arm roles

> **PHASE B-3 ÔÇö the ammunition economy on the real-time field ÔÇö is complete** (DECISIONS **D66**). New `src/tactical/T4-logistics.js` + guarded T0 seams + the Bull Run `supply` block + `tools/probe-logistics.mjs`. Deliverable Ôëł**1608KB**.
>
> **Ôťů B-3 ÔÇö supply trains + resupply + exhaustion:** each side fields a rear **ammunition train** with a finite **reserve**; a DISENGAGED brigade within reach refills (draining the reserve); a brigade OUT of cartridges holding the objective fires dry Ôćĺ bayonet (the 20th Maine); a SPENT brigade (fatigue>84) drags. The **attacker's train sits far behind its start line** (it outruns its supply) and the **defender's just behind the objective** Ôćĺ balance-neutral. **Ties strategic supply:** the reserve scales with `bridgeArmy().supply`; a raid-supply order cuts the enemy's. Gated + BYTE-IDENTICAL behind `__FIELD.logistics` (the 7 baselines + officers set sticky `_logisticsOff`).
>
> **THE FOG FIX (the headline ÔÇö a HIGH bug-hunt finding, surfaced to Aaron):** with **fog ON**, logistics first INVERTED "fog aids the defender" (D58/D64) ÔÇö Bull Run AI-vs-AI fog-ON **CS 8/8 Ôćĺ 0/8** (under fog the attacker cycled fresh brigades to its safe far-rear train and out-sustained the long fire-trade). Aaron's first pick (a defender's-depot rule) provably did nothing (the defender wasn't the ammo-constrained side); the fix that works (Aaron-approved) is **choking the ATTACKER's resupply under fog** (`ATK_FOG_RESUPPLY`=0 ÔÇö an attacker advancing blind can't run its trains forward). **Result: logistics is balance-NEUTRAL in BOTH fog states ÔÇö fog-OFF CS 5/8, fog-ON CS 8/8** (each = the no-logistics baseline; fog-aids-defender preserved). A FOG REGRESSION GUARD probe step locks it.
>
> **Ôťů FULLY VETTED:** adversarial bug-hunt **64 agents Ôćĺ 9 confirmed + 2 critic gaps, ALL ADDRESSED** (1 HIGH fog + 6 LOW probe-fidelity/correctness: probe boundary test, two-sided balance band, asymmetry + fog-reveal + supply-curve probe steps, reinforcement-only-side train). **probe-logistics 14/14, 0 pe** ┬Ě full no-regression GREEN (7 baselines byte-identical ┬Ě bootprobe ok ┬Ě t1probe 14/14 ┬Ě diag-classic 346) ┬Ě wcag clean (1 HUD-contrast fix). Committed + pushed.

Turn on Fog (V) and the defender still holds the hill ÔÇö the attacker outruns its supply.

## 1 ┬Ě THE PROJECT IN ONE PARAGRAPH
"The Civil War" is becoming **the definitive teaching wargame: Ultimate General: Gettysburg's combat FEEL + Paradox-grade strategic DEPTH + a museum's historical RIGOR** ÔÇö all three, no compromise. You are the **President (Lincoln or Davis)** running the entire war (economy, politics, diplomacy, morale, generals, the home front) AND commanding the battles in a real-time, gridless, drag-to-maneuver tactical engine ÔÇö wrapped in a PhD-level history + alternate-history teaching layer where scholarly consensus is the *favored-but-not-guaranteed* path. **The governing design law (Aaron's central tension, resolved): the simple low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun CORE that stands alone; ALL depth is optional ÔÇö auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able; education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real in-game mastery (so learning and fun pull the SAME direction).** One engine must serve the pure-battle player, the grand-strategist, and the PhD-historian simultaneously.

## 2 ┬Ě WHERE THINGS STAND (run h, verified)
- **Classic (hex, turn-based) is FROZEN/finished** ÔÇö the complete hex lineage + its 3D-skin "Modern." NEVER regress it (`tools/diag-classic.mjs` every splice).
- **Shipped + GPU-verified this run (all reusable):** procedural unit motion; **131 real PD-photo leader portraits** (`assets/portraits/`, license-gated, side-split for Anderson/Gregg) with a closure refactor + upgraded engraving fallback; a fuller period UI pass (drawn order-icons, engraved frames, brass portrait mat). Plus the inherited cinematic 3D foundation (PBR terrain, HDRI, ACES/bloom post-FX, weather, props, camera) and the adaptive period audio score.
- **The shipped "Modern" is only a 3D re-skin of the hex-turn engine** ÔÇö it does NOT play like UG:G. The real-time tactical engine + the grand-strategy owner-mode are **NOT built yet** ÔÇö that's the next work.
- **DESIGN: 63 decisions LOCKED** across a 35-round popup design session (Aaron). Fully captured in `GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN.md` (Parts IÔÇôIII). **No new-engine code written yet** ÔÇö the next chat builds from the spec.

## 3 ┬Ě THE DOCS (read in this order ÔÇö you have zero prior context)

## 4 ┬Ě ARCHITECTURE DECISION (run h ÔÇö important)
**Modularize via a zero-dependency build step.** The scope (50ÔÇô100k+ lines) outgrows the single 14k-line file. Author the new engine in **source modules**; a tiny **node concat script** assembles the one shippable `civil_war_generals.html` (keep the $0/portable/open-and-play deliverable + `play.command`). Set this up FIRST in S0. Classic + the existing engine stay intact through the transition (move them into the build later, carefully, or keep the current HTML as the base the build appends to). Gate the BUILT output (parse/hex/Classic-regression). This replaces the append-only-single-file splice model for new work ÔÇö but the gate discipline carries over.

## 5 ┬Ě BUILD ORDER & PHASES (Aaron: STRATEGIC-FIRST, confirmed twice)
**Phase group S (grand-strategy owner-mode) FIRST, then phase group P (real-time tactical).** Battles use the EXISTING engine via a clean bridge until the UG:G engine swaps in.
- **S0 ÔÇö scaffold:** set up the module/build system; expand the War Department (`G.campaign.{clock,muster,warroom}`) into the President's-desk shell (period war-room UI); strategic-turn loop; save. Layered scenario onboarding (start ~1861, limited toolset).
- **S1 ÔÇö economy** (full asymmetric model + finance/inflation/blockade).
- **S2 ÔÇö executive decisions + 3-layer morale + the 1864 election; the advisor/cabinet system** (the linchpin: auto-manage + recommend + TEACH, per-domain delegation).
- **S3 ÔÇö alt-history engine** (tiered divergence + hinge-points + emergent toggle + curated scenarios; deterministic-by-performance with consensus framing; the "your war vs history" tracker).
- **S4 ÔÇö education layer** (multi-voice debate cards + deep-dives + codex from HISTORICAL-DATA.md; ambient teaching; difficulty/realism sliders; play-style presets; full a11y).
- **S5 ÔÇö victory/defeat** (asymmetric paths incl. **negotiated peace for both sides**, military-only hard-loss) + all campaign scopes; wire existing battles through the bridge Ôćĺ **playable full owner-mode war.**
- **THEN P0ÔÇôP5** (`MODERN-UGG-PLAN.md`): the real-time UG:G tactical engine (First Bull Run vertical slice first), swapping in behind the bridge.
Each phase: gate + real-GPU self-verify (probes you READ) + Classic no-regression + left in a working, polished state (ship-quality iteratively).

## 6 ┬Ě THE BALANCE PRINCIPLE (design law ÔÇö apply to EVERY system)
The simple, low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun core that works on its own. Every deep system is optional ÔÇö auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able mid-campaign. Education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real mastery (learning is rewarded by winning, not a chore-score). Presets + sliders let each player set their own balance. **If a feature forces depth on a battle-first player, it's wrong; if it denies depth to a strategist/historian, it's wrong.** (Full statement: GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN ┬ž27.)

## 7 ┬Ě TOOLCHAIN, GATES, GOTCHAS (proven ÔÇö reuse)
- **Gates every change:** `.bak` Ôćĺ parse (`node --check` the built/extracted `<script>`) Ôćĺ invalid-hex grep `0x[0-9a-fA-F]*[g-z]` = 0 Ôćĺ collision-grep new fns = 0. With the new build step, gate the assembled output.
- **Real-GPU self-verify (READ the PNGs/probes):** `tools/shot-postfx.mjs`, `tools/shot-gpu.mjs`, `tools/shot-ui.mjs`, `tools/probe-motion.mjs`, `tools/probe-portraits.mjs`, `tools/bootprobe.mjs`, `tools/diag-classic.mjs`. Real GPU = **Intel UHD 617** via headed Chrome `--use-angle=metal`. A real-time sim/strategic loop needs an EMPIRICAL probe (sample state over frames), not just screenshots. Stale server: `lsof -ti tcp:8765 | xargs kill`.
- **Perf target:** smooth on the Intel UHD 617 at Auto tier; instancing/LOD/perf-tiers mandatory.
- **CRITICAL gotchas:** `G`/`HEX`/`PALETTE`/`THREE_BASE` are bare-name lexical globals (never `window.G`); THREE loads async (no top-level `new THREE.*`); override-by-redeclaration (last def wins); never a literal `*/` in a block comment; honor `reduceMotion` + `gfxQuality`; **NEVER regress Classic**; $0/free-CC0; Verified/Inferred provenance on all history.
- **Asset pipeline (historical run-H note; current top block supersedes live setup):** PD images via the run-h portrait pattern (Wikipedia REST summary Ôćĺ Commons license API PD-gate Ôćĺ download Ôćĺ `sips` resize). Extend to weapons/flags/USCT. Blender MCP remains available for future explicit 3D asset jobs (PolyHaven CC0 / Sketchfab), but Blender does not need to stay open unless a Phase-H asset task starts; free Hyper3D trial is drained.
